							<p><strong><span style="font-size: medium">
							Welcome 
							to VPN Gate.</span><span style="color: #008000"> 
							(Launched on March 8, 2013.)</span></strong><br />
							<strong><span style="font-size: medium">
							<a href="http://www.softether.org/">
							<img height="86" src="images/sevpn_30.jpg" style="float: right" width="451" /></a></span></strong>- 
							You can get through your government&#39;s firewall to browse 
							restricted websites. (e.g. YouTube.)<br />
							- You can disguise your IP address to hide your
							identity while surfing the Internet.<br />
							- You can protect yourself by utilizing the 
							strong encryption while using public Wi-Fi.
							<a href="about_overview.aspx">More 
							Details...</a></p>
							<p>Supports <a href="howto_windows.aspx">Windows</a>,
							<a href="howto_mac.aspx">Mac</a>,
							<a href="howto_ios.aspx">iPhone</a>,
							<a href="howto_ios.aspx">iPad</a> and
							<a href="howto_android.aspx">Android</a>.</p>
							<p style="text-align: right">
							<a href="http://www.softether.org/"><strong>VPN Gate 
							is based on SoftEther VPN, a multi-protocol VPN 
							server.</strong></a><br />
							</p>

					<p>&nbsp;</p>
					<a name="LIST"></a>
					<p style="text-align: center;">
					<span style="font-size: 13pt;"><strong>
					The <span id="Label_Num">6423</span> Public VPN Relay Servers 
					by volunteers 
					around the world.<br />
					</strong>
					<span style="color: #0000AA">You may connect to any of these 
					VPN servers with: Username: 'vpn', Password: 'vpn'.</span></span></p>
					<p>
						Apply search filters:
						<span style="font-weight:normal;"><input id="C_SoftEther" type="checkbox" name="C_SoftEther" checked="checked" /><label for="C_SoftEther">SoftEther VPN (SSL-VPN)</label></span>
&nbsp;
						<span style="font-weight:normal;"><input id="C_L2TP" type="checkbox" name="C_L2TP" checked="checked" /><label for="C_L2TP">L2TP/IPsec</label></span>
&nbsp;
						<span style="font-weight:normal;"><input id="C_OpenVPN" type="checkbox" name="C_OpenVPN" checked="checked" /><label for="C_OpenVPN">OpenVPN</label></span>
&nbsp;
						<span style="font-weight:normal;"><input id="C_SSTP" type="checkbox" name="C_SSTP" checked="checked" /><label for="C_SSTP">MS-SSTP</label></span>
&nbsp;
						<input type="submit" name="Button3" value="Refresh Servers List" id="Button3" style="font-family:Arial;font-weight:normal;width:190px;" />
						&nbsp;<a href="join.aspx">(Add your VPN server to this list.)</a><br />
						<span style="color: #008000"><strong>You must specify the IP 
						address of the destination VPN Server, instead of DDNS 
						hostname (.opengw.net) if you are under censorship. 
						</strong></span></p>
					<p>
						Do you want to parse the below HTML table? Instead you 
						can use <strong><a href="/api/iphone/">CSV List</a></strong> 
						to make your own VPN Gate client app.</p>

							In order to prevent DoS attacks we show only some portion 
							of available servers.<br />

					<p style="text-align: center; font-size: medium;">
							<strong><span style="color: #FF0000">Warning for 
							Censorship Firewall Authorities</span><br />
							</strong>Using the VPN Server List of VPN Gate 
							Service as the IP Blocking List of your country&#39;s 
							Censorship Firewall is prohibited by us.<br />
							The VPN Server List sometimes contains wrong IP 
							addresses.<br />
							If you enter the IP address list into your 
							Censorship Firewall, unexpected accidents will occur 
							on the firewall.<br />
							Therefore you must not use the VPN Server List for 
							managing your Censorship Firewall&#39;s IP blocking 
							list.</p>
					<p style="text-align: right">
							&nbsp;</p>
					<p>A VPN Server with higher Line Speed (measured by Mbps) and smaller Ping result are usually more comfortable to use. You might be able to browse websites which are normally unreachable from your area if you use VPN servers that are not in your area.</p>
